"Pieris rapae","2015-04-09 14:15:00 -0700","This is a Cabbage White butterfly (Pieris rapae) that I photographed while out on my bi-weekly <a href=""http://research.nhm.org/bioscan/bioscanbuzz/?p=652"" rel=""nofollow"">ButterflySCAN</a> outing. ButterflySCAN is a <a href=""http://www.nhm.org/site/activities-programs/citizen-science"" rel=""nofollow"">Citizen Science</a> project of the <a href=""https://www.nhm.org"" rel=""nofollow"">Los Angeles County Natural History Museum</a>.

For the ButterflySCAN project, I have been assigned a location to explore every two weeks. My site is called Solano Canyon and is located northwest of downtown Los Angeles. (I enjoy this activity so much that sometimes I go every week, or every week-and-a-half, rather than waiting the full two weeks.) During my outing I walk through the neighborhood looking for, and counting, the various butterflies that I encounter. I also try to get photos of the butterflies that I see. For the ButterflySCAN project, I have been assigned a location to explore every two weeks. My site is called Solano Canyon and is located northwest of downtown Los Angeles.
